<review>Beautiful! Great place!
To use the parking area you need an Adventure Pass. This is 4.5 mile hike in (9 round trip) from the trailhead to the falls. The path itself is single walker wide with with a good bit of elevation change. There are areas where a slip could cause a fall of several hundred feet and surly, mortality. And, areas with less extreme but certainly potentially fatal falls could occur. Please beware with small children! The path itself is mostly not difficult to navigate though there are a few areas where you are going to need to be able walk across 100% rocky areas. And be prepared for large rocks all along the path. You will need to be aware. As well, there is the potential for Mountain Lions and Rattlesnake so, take appropriate precautions. When we went, we passed 5 or 6 other parties so, it's not completely unknown. Still, most wouldn't want to try and navigate this area in the dark and there is no cellular service.<//review>< pics>
None< /pics>

< Text>
Yes, to all those wondering, this is officially Boba Guys. This location essentially serves as their storage/test kitchen as well? so the menu is also limited in terms of the variety of drinks available. Nonetheless, after trying some more other places recently, I've affirmed my realization that it has the best quality and taste milk tea.

Very easy to place and order on their square site and pick it up.< /Text>

< review>
Boba Guys but under a different name. Can't complain! Easier than going into the city.

We came here today as we were very hungry and this was the first place we came up on. We walked in and no one greeted us but there were people in the restaurant so we just seated ourselves. We ordered our drinks a few minutes after we sat down. The gentleman brought us chips and salsa. The chips tasted stale and the salsa was pretty bland. My husband got his beer before I got my diet coke. I didn't get my drink until almost 10 minutes later. We were able to order maybe 10 minutes after that. My husband got a burrito and I got enchiladas. His burrito was bland as well. My tortilla and cheese for the enchilada was good but the red sauce was a bit thick and bland as well. There was no spice to it at all. It was sweet too which was weird. The rice was mushy but the beans were great, I wish the whole meal was like that. The gentleman assisting us I believe was the owner. He did not come to check on us. He seemed to be more involved with the soccer game and looking at his phone. The service was subpar to say the least. The lady working there was nice though.< /review>
